// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            $('[id="Consignee Name Address"]').on('keydown', $('[id="Consignee Name Address"]').find("input[name='code']"), function(e) { 
                var keyCode = e.keyCode || e.which; 

                if (keyCode == 9) { 
                    e.preventDefault(); 
                    // look up the address on tab
                    $('[caption="Consignee Name Address"]').find('button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').click();
                } 
            });
        });
    }

// Source: AGCS (ffund)_Fireman's Fund Reference Configuration Rule_21.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
        //retreive custom user data for Shipper Reference based on CustomData key 
        var customValue = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);  //this.GetShipment(shipmentRequest).UserRef1;
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = customValue;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = customValue;
    };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        
        //create value for Shipper Reference (Ex: CustomData Reference1Value)
        var ref1Value = this.CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);
        //var customValue = this.CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20);
        var customValue = this.CheckReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference);
        var referenceValue = customValue + " " + ref1Value;
        
        
        //set the above value for each package in the shipment
        for(var i = 0;i<shipmentRequest.Packages.length;i++){
           shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = referenceValue;
        }
        
        //check the user custom data against the validation list; if the value is not in the list, don't ship and produce an error
        this.CheckValidation(customValue, this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.FieldOptionValidations);
    };

    };

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = thisShipper;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = thisBatchName;
    };

// function SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration() // returns undefined
function SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration()
	{		
		
		SetDescription('Returned Goods');	
		//SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail('');
		SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(true,undefined);
		//$('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val();
		LoadReturnAddressFromShipperAddress("SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration()");	
	}

// function SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(enabled, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(enabled = false,shipmentRequest)
	{		
		debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest != undefined && enabled == true)
		{			
			if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country.toUpperCase() != USCOUNTRY) 
				&& (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country.toUpperCase() != USACRONYM))
			{
				$('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected",true);				
			}
			else	
			{
				$('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected",false);			}
		}
	}

// function OnShipperChange(currentShipper) // returns undefined
function OnShipperChange(currentShipper)
		{		
		SwitchOnOffD2MShipment("OnShipperChange()");
		
		var cond1 = CurrentShipmentIsD2M();
		var cond2 = CurrentSessionIsCapableOfD2MShipments();
		var cond3 = currentShipper === LINCONLSHIRE_D2M_SHIPPER;
		
	    if(( cond1 || cond2 ) && cond3)
	    {					
			SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration();				
	    }
	    else
		{
			ClearReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration();								
		}	    	}

// function ClearReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration() // returns undefined
function ClearReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration()
	{		
		
		SetDescription('');
		SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail('');
		SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(false,undefined);	
		$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].CommercialInvoiceMethod"]').val('');
		//ClearAllSelect();
	}

         return shipmentRequest;
    }

        $saveShipmentProfileModal = angular.element('#saveShipmentProfileModal');
        $saveShipmentProfileModal.on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShippingProfile"]').focus();
            });
        $deleteShipmentProfileModal = angular.element('#deleteShipmentProfileModal');
        $processEODModal = angular.element('#processEODModal');
        
        vm.showSaveShippingProfileModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $saveShipmentProfileModal.modal('show');
            }

        vm.showDeleteShippingProfileModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $deleteShipmentProfileModal.modal('show');
            }
        
        vm.saveShippingProfile = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            var selsvc = this.selectedServices[0].Symbol;
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'S';
            shipmentRequest.ShippingProfileName = vm.currentShippingProfile;
            shipmentRequest.SelService = selsvc;
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var curprofilelist = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                vm.shippingProfiles = curprofilelist;
                })
            
            $saveShipmentProfileModal.modal('hide');
            }

        vm.deleteShippingProfile = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'D';
            shipmentRequest.ShippingProfileName = vm.currentShippingProfile;
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var curprofilelist = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                vm.shippingProfiles = curprofilelist;
                })
            
            $deleteShipmentProfileModal.modal('hide');
            }

        vm.shippingProfileChange = function (shipmentRequest)
            {
            var tmpShippingProfile = vm.shippingProfiles.find(({ ShippingProfileName }) => ShippingProfileName === this.currentShippingProfile);
            var newShippingProfile = structuredClone(tmpShippingProfile);    
            if( newShippingProfile !== null && newShippingProfile !== undefined) {
                var selsvc = newShippingProfile.SelService;
                var myservice = {Symbol: selsvc };
                if( newShippingProfile.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery === true) {
                    newShippingProfile.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions = [4096,2048,32];                    
                }

                var today = new Date();
                var curdate = {Year: today.getFullYear(), Month: today.getMonth() + 1, Day: today.getDate()};
                newShippingProfile.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = curdate;
                this.currentShipment = newShippingProfile;
                this.selectedServices[0] = myservice;
                }
            }

        vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function ()
            {
            vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DirectDelivery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Proof = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignature = false; 
            vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.2DA" };
            if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                vm.selectedServices = [];
            }
            vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };

        vm.showProcessEODModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $processEODModal.modal('show');
            }

        vm.ProcessEOD = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'EOD';
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var eodresult = ret.Data;
                $processEODModal.modal('hide');                
                })
            }

        }

// Source: AlstonBird (ALBI)_ClientBusinessRules_1866.cs
// function importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(checked) // returns void
        function importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(checked) {
            if (checked) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = {
                    Company: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company,
                    Contact: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact,
                    Address1: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1,
                    Address2: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address2,
                    Address3: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address3,
                    City: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.City,
                    StateProvince: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince,
                    PostalCode: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PostalCode,
                    Country: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country
                }
            } else {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = {}
            }
        }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.shipping ??= client.setMailroomOrTraveler(this.vm.profile.Name);
        if (this.vm.shipping.IsMailroom) client.shipping.loadValue.focus();        
        client.shipping.consignee.updateStateProvince(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults?.Consignee?.Country);
        
        if (this.vm.shipping.IsTraveler) {
            this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
            this.vm.createLicensePlateButtonCaption = 'Get Rate'
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = client.userName;
        } 
        this.vm.validateClientMatter = this.validateClientMatter;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = client.userName;        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = client.userName;        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = client.userName;  
        // shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference = '040614-548313';
    }

// Source: AMERICAN INTERNATIONAL GROUP (AIG)_Shipper Ref = Custom1_25.cs
// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         //retreive custom user data for Shipper Reference based on CustomData key 
        var customValue;
        var CustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        
        for(var Custom in CustomData){
            if(CustomData[Custom].Key=="Custom1")customValue = CustomData[Custom].Value;
        }
       
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = customValue;
       
    }

// Source: Amplifon (AMPN)_Amplifon CBR_1917.cs
// function InitShipment(calleeMethod) // returns void
    function InitShipment(calleeMethod)
    {
        debugger;
        console.log ("Info: InitShipment called by: " + calleeMethod);
        
         if (location.hash === '#!/shipping') 
         {
            var currentShipper = vm?.currentShipment?.PackageDefaults?.Shipper;
            
            if (currentShipper!=undefined && currentShipper != "MNHQ")
            {
                LoadCostCenter(); 
				var originAddressCompany,isLoaded;
                var originAddressLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
                originAddressCompany = $('[name="company"]:eq(2)').val();
                if (originAddressCompany!=undefined && originAddressCompany.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(originAddressLoadedInterval);	
                    CopyOriginAddressToReturnAddress();
                }
            },50);
            }
        }
    }

// function CopyOriginAddressToReturnAddress() // returns void
    function CopyOriginAddressToReturnAddress()
    {
        debugger;
        var currentUserOriginAddress = vm?.profile?.UserInformation?.Address;
        
        if (currentUserOriginAddress !== undefined && $.isEmptyObject(currentUserOriginAddress) ===false)
        {
            vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = currentUserOriginAddress;
            console.log ("User Origin Address to Return Address : OK");
        }
        else
        {
             console.log ("Error: Origin Address not found");
        }
    }

// function LoadCostCenter() // returns void
    function LoadCostCenter()
    {
        var currentUserData = vm?.profile?.UserInformation?.Address.CustomData;
        var costCenter = GetUserData(currentUserData, "CostCenter");
        if ($.isEmptyObject(costCenter) === false)
        {
             console.log ("CostCenter detected: " + JSON.stringify(costCenter));
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference = costCenter.Value;
             $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').prop( "disabled", true );
        }
        else
        {
            console.log ("Error: CostCenter not found");
        }
    }

// this.GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
    this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// Source: Asia Waterjet FZCO (ASIAWATERJETFZCO)_Asia_WaterJet_CBR_1870.cs
// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        var freightfound = 0;
        var frieghterr = 0;

        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) >= 70) {
                freightfound = "1";
            }
            if (freightfound == "1") {
                if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) < 70) {
                    frieghterr = "1";
                }
            }
        }
        if (freightfound == "0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR"
            }
        } else {
            if (frieghterr == "0") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                    Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT"
                }
            } else {
                alert("Cannot create one shipment with 2 different service levels.");
            }
        }
        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol == "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT") {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Packaging = "CUSTOMER_PALLET";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ImportDelivery = true;

        }
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country == "US") {
            if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == '?') {
                alert("Please confirm shipment value");
                throw ("Excpetion");
            } else {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == "") {
                    if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == 'string:Yes') {
                        alert("Please Enter ITN/ EES number in ConsigneeReference");
                        throw ("Excpetion");
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country != "undefined") {
                alert("For EU Exports : Shipments above 1000 EUR, a formal export declaration is required. A formal electronic export declaration must be sent to customs authorities by the exporter or their representative. Customs authorities grant the release for export and issue an Export Accompanying Document (EAD) with a unique Movement Reference Number (MRN). The EAD has to accompany the shipment. UPS is responsible for the exit clearance at the EU border.")
            }
        }
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston Coyol Client Business Rules_2474.cs
// function ShippingLoaded() // returns undefined
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

   // debugger;
   
    if(SelectedReturnAddress !== undefined && SelectedReturnAddress !== null){
         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {

            Company : SelectedReturnAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedReturnAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address2,
            Address3 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address3,
            City : SelectedReturnAddress.City,
            StateProvince : SelectedReturnAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedReturnAddress.PostalCode,
            Country : SelectedReturnAddress.Country,
            Email : SelectedReturnAddress.Email,
            Phone : SelectedReturnAddress.Phone
        };
    }
};

// function AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
     //debugger;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
    //shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SedMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod;

}

// function GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
    function GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        if (customDataType === "To") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                if (fieldName.toUpperCase() === customField.Key.toUpperCase()) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;
    }

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// Source: Cabinet Works Group (MASCO)_Masco Client Side Business Rules_1752.cs
// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}


// Source: Carrier Misroute (CMR) (CMR)_Client Business Rules_2487.cs
// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        thinClient.loading.show();
        thinClient.dismiss.All();
        userParams.customer = this.vm.shipping.customer.value;
        userParams.labelImage = this.vm.labelImage;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15 = thinClient.today();
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        thinClient.loading.hide();
        this.vm.labelImage = null;


        if (this.vm.shipping.customer.value == 'AMAZON') {
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ConsigneeReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = true;

            if (this.vm.loadValue == 'Return') {
                this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = false;
                //this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
            }
        }

        if((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option')) {
            this.vm.shipping.activePanel = 0;
            this.vm.shipping.panelMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
        }
        this.vm.loadValue = null;
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function(shipmentRequest) {
 
      var shipment = GetShipment(shipmentRequest);

      shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (packageItem) {
         packageItem.ShipperReference = shipment.UserRef1;
         packageItem.ConsigneeReference = shipment.UserRef4;
      });

      function GetShipment(shipmentRequest) {

         class Shipment {
            constructor(shipmentRequest) {
               this.ShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
            }

            get UserRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User"); }
            get UserRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User"); }
            get UserRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User"); }
            get UserRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "User"); }
            get UserRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "User"); }
            get UserRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "User"); }
            get UserRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "User"); }
            get UserRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "User"); }
            get UserRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "User"); }
            get UserRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "User"); }

            get ToRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "To"); }
            get ToRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "To"); }
            get ToRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "To"); }
            get ToRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "To"); }
            get ToRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "To"); }
            get ToRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "To"); }
            get ToRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "To"); }
            get ToRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "To"); }
            get ToRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "To"); }
            get ToRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "To"); }

            GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
               var returnValue = "";
               var customData = null;
               if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
               if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

               if (customData) {
                  customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                     if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
                  })
               }
               return returnValue;
            }
         }
         return new Shipment(shipmentRequest);
      }
   };

           GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        
        console.log('new shipment!');
        
        //Set the variable below equal to the name of the Custom Data field for this company
        var customDataName1 = "Custom1";
        var customDataName2 = "Custom2";
        
        var customSFValue1;
        var customSFValue2;
        
        var CustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        for(var SFCustom in CustomData){
            if(CustomData[SFCustom].Key==customDataName1)customSFValue1 = CustomData[SFCustom].Value;
            if(CustomData[SFCustom].Key==customDataName2)customSFValue2 = CustomData[SFCustom].Value;
        }
        
        var ref1;
        var ref2;
        
        //if null or undefined, set reference values to empty
        if(!customSFValue1)customSFValue1 = "";
        if(!customSFValue2)customSFValue2 = "";
        
        
        ref1 = customSFValue2;
        ref2 = customSFValue1;
        
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = ref1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = ref2;
    
        // Default Delivery Notification email to active user
		var userEmail = getUserEmail();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotification = true;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        
    };

// Source: CNH_DEALER CONNECT (CNH)_CNH Billing Rule_74.cs
// SelectBillingOption(nameAddress, shipmentRequest) // returns void
function SelectBillingOption(nameAddress, shipmentRequest){
        var customName1 = "Custom1";
        var customName2 = "Custom2";
        var customValue1, customValue2;
        var CustomSTData = nameAddress.CustomData;
        //alert(CustomSTData.length);
       
        try{
            for(var Custom in CustomSTData){
                if(CustomSTData[Custom]){
                    if(CustomSTData[Custom].Key==customName1)customValue1 = CustomSTData[Custom].Value;
                    if(CustomSTData[Custom].Key==customName2)customValue2 = CustomSTData[Custom].Value;
                }
            }
        }catch(err){
            throw({message:"Unable to get billing data", number:"001"});
        }
        //alert(customValue1);
        if(customValue2 != "PP"){
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            nameAddress.Account = customValue1;
        }
    }

// Source: Coach (Coach)_Coach Business Rule_20.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
function ClientBusinessRules() {
    
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         //retreive custom user data for Shipper Reference based on CustomData key 
        var customValue;
        var CustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        
        for(var Custom in CustomData){
            if(CustomData[Custom].Key=="Custom1")customValue = CustomData[Custom].Value;
        }
       
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customValue;
       
    }
}

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (cbr.historyShipment != null) {
            var historyRequest = JSON.parse(cbr.historyShipment);
            this.vm.totalPackages = historyRequest.Packages.length;

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults = historyRequest.PackageDefaults;
            shipmentRequest.Packages = historyRequest.Packages;
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Description = "PC Equipment";

            shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
                pkg.ReturnDelivery = true;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = historyRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
                pkg.Description = "PC Equipment";
            });
            cbr.historyShipment = null;
        }
        cbr.bulk.create.itemReferences = [];
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// function PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// function PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        var stName;
        var vmExists = false;

        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");

        if (typeof objVM === "undefined") {
            stName = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        } else {
            vmExists = true;
            stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            objVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = isDefined(customData2) + "~" + stName;
        }
        // alert("customData2 = " + customData2);


        if (isDefined(customData3) == "FC") {
            if (vmExists === true) {
                objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            } else {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            }
            nameaddress.Account = isDefined(customData1);
        }

        function PullCustomData(consignee, field) {
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));

            for (var item in consignee) {
                if (consignee[item].Key == field) return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }

        function isDefined(referenceValue) {
            var goodValue = null;
            if (typeof referenceValue == "undefined" ||
                referenceValue === null) {
                goodValue = "";
            } else {
                goodValue = referenceValue;
            }
            return goodValue;
        }
    };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod !== null &&
            typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod !== "undefined") shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "SHIPPER";
    };

// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
            // Updates code to get UserId from the vm instead of an API call
            pkg.MiscReference20 = vm.UserInformation.UserId;  
        });

        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            var sfState = getStateAbbreviation(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince);
            if (sfState !== null &&
                typeof sfState !== "undefined") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = sfState;
            }
        }
    };

// AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns undefined
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = getShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
        function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
    function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
    function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) // returns emailAddress object
    function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) {
        var emailAddress = {}
        if (def.Consignee.Email != undefined && def.Consignee.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Consignee = def.Consignee.Email;
        }
        if (def.OriginAddress != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Origin = def.OriginAddress.Email;
        }
        return emailAddress;
    }

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        
        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");
        
        var stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        
        if(customData3=="FC"){
            objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            nameaddress.Account = customData1;
        }
        
        
        function PullCustomData(consignee, field){
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));
            
            for(var item in consignee){
                if(consignee[item].Key==field)return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.consigneeCountryChange = this.ConsigneeCountryChange;
        var originCustomData = getCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = getKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = getKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
        setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee);
    };

// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince = getStateAbbreviation(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince);
//	debugger;
        //var branchNo = getKeyValue('Custom3', userCustomData)
		
		var branchNo = client.getValueByKey('Custom3', this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData);
		
        var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
        for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
            packages[i].MiscReference20 = branchNo;
            if (this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ProofRequireSignature || this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ProofRequireSignatureAdult) {
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Proof = true;
            }
            else {
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Proof = false;
            }
        }
    };

// setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns undefined
    function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
        var isInternational = nameAddress.Country != 'US';
        $('[property="Packaging"] select').prop('disabled', isInternational);
        if (isInternational) {
            var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
            for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
                packages[i].Packaging = 'LETTER';
            }
        }
    }

  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {

    if (location == '/shipping')
    {
      $(function()
      {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val('DOCUMENTS');
        $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"]').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'blur', function(e)
        {
          $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"] button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
        });
      });
    }

    if (location == '/batchmanager')
    {
      console.log(this.vm);
      console.log(this);
      $(document).ready(function()
      {
        $.globalEval('var userContext;');

        $('#batchUpdateTabs').delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
        {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopImmediatePropagation();
          e.stopPropagation();

          var i = $(this).attr('index');
          UIMethods.SwitchToTab(i);
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', function(e)
        {
          $(this).removeClass('has-error');
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkEditBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.EditThisBatch(this);
        });

        $('body').delegate('#checkboxthirdparty', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CheckForThirdPartyBilling();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.UpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCancelBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CancelUpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

      });
    }
  }

          {

          }

          /* Don Beal (dbeal@ups.com) - 2021-12-09 */

          // /* Validate the address, this is only needed for 7F4175 and 8942X4 */

// CheckWeightAndService(weightVal) // returns undefined
  function CheckWeightAndService (weightVal)
  {
    // /* Once the button is clicked, start a timer and wait for the weight to populate. */
    // /* If the weight is over 1 pound, switch the service from USPS FC to UPS Ground. */
    if ((weightVal > 1) && ($('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').find('option:selected').val() == "CONNECTSHIP_ENDICIA.USPS.FIRST"))
    {

      /* Deselect any currently selected options. */
      $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').val([]).scrollTop(10);

      /* Select the ground option. */
      $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"] > option[value="CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND"]')
        .prop({ 'selected': 'true', 'selected': true })
        .attr('selected', 'selected')
        .trigger('change').promise().done(function ()
        {

        });
    }
  }

// ShowLoader() // returns undefined
  function ShowLoader ()
  {
    $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-hide').addClass('ng-show');
  }

// HideLoader() // returns undefined
  function HideLoader ()
  {
    $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-show').addClass('ng-hide');
  }

// GetWeightFromScale(callback) // returns undefined
  function GetWeightFromScale(callback)
  {
    $('[ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function()
    {
      /* Set the default box type to 'BAG 1'.  The multiple props and attr are for older browsers. */
      if ($.isFunction(callback)) callback;
    });
  }

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderNumber) // returns undefined
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function(OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString).trigger('change');
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString).trigger('change');
      }

  }

        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
         
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

// TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressChange() // returns undefined

        debugger;

        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress;

// SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();
		
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
	
		//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
        //this.vm.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
		
        //this.vm.overrideOptimization = pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6)
        pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6);
		
		//checkAndSetShipDate(this.vm);
		checkAndSetShipDateTest(this.vm);
		
        this.vm.arriveByDate = client.shipping.arriveByDate;
        client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();

        function pastDueDate(miscReference6) {
            //if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0 && miscReference6 != '*1900-01-01T00:00:00*') {

            if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0) {

                miscReference6 = miscReference6.replaceAll('*', '');
                client.shipping.arriveByDate = miscReference6.split("T")[0];

                var dateRequired = Date.parse(miscReference6);
                if (dateRequired <= Date.now() && miscReference6 != "1900-01-01T00:00:00") {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-success').addClass('text-danger');
                    return true;
                }
                else {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').addClass('text-success');
                }
            };
            return false;
        }

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

		function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 6;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						//var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
						viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
						shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
						//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
			
			console
            return date;
        }
		
		function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;
			var hardCutoffTime = 16;
			var currentDateTime = new Date();
			var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();
			
			if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
				var finalDate = addDays(2);
				console.log("New date" + finalDate);
				var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
			}
			
		}

				console.log("New date" + finalDate);

				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
			}
			
		}

            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
               //Address 4
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "200 Terminal St.")

                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
