// ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
ShowAssignGoodsPane()
    {
      let that = this;

      //get rid of any previous entries
      $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

      //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
      //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
      $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

      //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
      this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;
      this.goods = this.json.data.map(m => m.boxes).flat();
      this.goods.sort((a, b) => { return a.skuId - b.skuId });

      //loop the commodities to create a master list item for each
      $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
        b.UniqueId = k;

        //copy the source element
        let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).data(b);

        //change the id of the main containing element so we don't run into issue later
        //each clone is a discreet list item which corresponds to a commodity
        $(item).attr('id', k);

        //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
        //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
        //let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

        $(item).find('.goods-sku').html('SKU: <strong>' + b.skuId + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('Quantity: <strong>' + b.quantity + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('Unit Cost: <strong>$' + b.unitPrice + '</strong>');

        //append it to our list
        $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

        //assign all goods to the first package
        that.packages[0].CommodityContents.push(that.GetCommodityContentObject(b));

        //update the weight and declared value in the root of the object
        let weight = that.packages[0].Weight;
        let dva = that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount;
        const thisWeight = (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs);
        const thisValue = (+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice);

        if (!weight.Amount) { weight.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].Weight.Amount += (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs).toFixed(2);

        if (!dva.Amount) { dva.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += Math.round((+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice) * 100) / 100;

        //show it gracefully
        $(item).show();
      });

      //that.UpdatePackageCounts();
      //$('li[heading=Goods] a:first').click();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
      $('.scan-input:visible').first().focus();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();
    }

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
   GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      
      if (customDataType === "User")
      {
          if(this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress)
          {
            customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
          }
      }
      
      if (customDataType === "To") 
      {
          if(this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee)
          {
            customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
          }
      }
      
      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }

class Shipment {
   constructor(shipmentRequest) {
      this.ShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
   }

 
   get UserEmail() { return this.GetEmail(); }

   get UserRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User"); }
   get UserRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User"); }
   get UserRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User"); }
   get UserRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "User"); }
   get UserRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "User"); }
   get UserRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "User"); }
   get UserRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "User"); }
   get UserRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "User"); }
   get UserRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "User"); }
   get UserRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "User"); }

   get ToRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "To"); }
   get ToRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "To"); }
   get ToRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "To"); }
   get ToRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "To"); }
   get ToRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "To"); }
   get ToRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "To"); }
   get ToRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "To"); }
   get ToRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "To"); }
   get ToRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "To"); }
   get ToRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "To"); }

   GetEmail(){
      var emailText = "";
      var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a"); 
      Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
         if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!","").trim(); 
      });
      return emailText;
   }
   
   GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
      if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }
// End Shipment Class    
}

        
         
}

// Source: Powder Valley (POWDER_VALLEY)_Powder Valley Client Business Rules_1658.cs
// myMethod() // returns void
function myMethod() {
        if ($('#ordersPerPage').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#ordersPerPage').val("10");
        }
        if ($('#pageNumber').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#pageNumber').val("1");
        }
        if ($('#dateAfter').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#dateAfter').val("2021-01-01");
        }
        if ($('#batchType').val().trim() === "" || $('#batchType').val().search("undefined") > -1) {
            $('#batchType').val("processing");
        }
    }

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns void
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) {
        /* This enables the button to edit the Third Party Billing Information. */
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', false).attr('disabled', false);

        /* Check the box for Third Party Billing which will bring up the modal.  Fill the modal with values.  Click Save. */
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', true).attr('checked', true).change();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {}
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = 'PRA Global';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = '995 Research Park Blvd';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = 'Suite 300';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = 'Charlottesville';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = 'VA';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = '22911';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = '883F79';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = 'US'
    }

// Source: Purolator (PURT)_PurolatorCBR_1906.cs
// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {     
        /**
        var date = new Date();
        var dateStr = date.getFullYear() + "-" + ("00" + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "-" + ("00" + date.getDate()).slice(-2);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateStr;
        
        var date = new Date();
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month = Number(date.getMonth() + 1);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day = Number(date.getDate());
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year = Number(date.getFullYear());
        */
        
        var date = new Date();
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month = Number(date.getMonth() + 1);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day = Number(date.getDate());
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year = Number(date.getFullYear());
        
        debugger;
        var brokerCode = "";
        for(var i=0; i<shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].DocumentsOnly === true)
            {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 0;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Description = 'Document Only';
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 1;
                //Commodities Description
                if (i == 0 && shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommodityContents)
                {
                    //debugger;
                    for (var indx = 0; indx < shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommodityContents.length; indx++)
                    {
                        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommodityContents[indx].Description)
                        {
                            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommodityContents[indx].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].CommodityContents[indx].Description.replace(/[\r\n\t]/g, "");
                        }
                    }
                }
                else                
                {
                    //alert("Missing Commodity Contents");
                }
            }

            //WorldEase Flag to assign to all packages
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].WorldEaseFlag = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].WorldEaseFlag;
            
            //WorldEase Additional Documents
            //debugger;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].AdditionalHardcopyDocumentation = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AdditionalHardcopyDocumentation;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ExportDeclarationStatement = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportDeclarationStatement;

            /**

// DefaultDangerousGoods() // returns void
    function DefaultDangerousGoods() {
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var divHaz = $('div[class="modal-dialog modal-lg"]');
            if (divHaz.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatCaCategory"]> option[value="number:3"]').prop('selected', true);
                $('select[ng-model="vm.hazmatContent.HazmatRegulationSet"]> option[value="number:2"]').prop('selected', true);
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// HidingDefaultShipDate() // returns void
    function HidingDefaultShipDate () {
        var date = new Date();
        var dateStr = date.getFullYear() + "-" + ("00" + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "-" + ("00" + date.getDate()).slice(-2);
        //debugger;
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var input = $('input[datepicker-options="vm.shipDateOptions"]');
            if (input.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                input.value(dateStr);
            }
        }, 50);
        
        
        
    }

// function PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === undefined) {
			alert("No service selected!");
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null  && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage === 'validate')
		{
			// click validate button
			$('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('button[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').click();
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(0, 4) === 'pop:') {
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== '')
		{
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}
		
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship')
		{
			if (!this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip) {
				this.vm.checkShip();
			}
		}
	};

// function PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== 0)
		{
			alert("Shipping error: " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode);
		}
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = false;    // signature_required_checkbox
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = true;    // autoship_checkbox
	};

// MyShipperChange() // returns undefined
this.MyShipperChange = function () {
        var shipmentRequest = this.currentShipment;
        var originName = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Name;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = originName ? shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Symbol : '';
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = originName ? shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince + "," + originName.split('(')[0] : '';
    }

// Source: Roadie XD (ROADIEXD)_Company Client Business Rules_2453.cs
// function ThirdPartyBillingDisabled(isDisabled) // returns undefined
        function thirdPartyBillingDisabled(isDisabled) {
            var $tpb = $('div[property="ThirdPartyBilling"]');
            if (isDisabled) {
                this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = false;
                this.thirdPartyBilling();
                $tpb.find('input').attr('disabled', true);
                $tpb.find('label').addClass('disabled');
            } else {
                $tpb.find('input').removeAttr('disabled');
                $tpb.find('label').removeClass('disabled');
            }
        }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function()

    {
		
		
        //Set Consignee Countries
        var consigneeCountries = ['', 'US', 'CA', 'AU']
        setConsigneeCountries(consigneeCountries);

        //Set Currency Options
        declaredValueCurrencyOptions();
        customsDeclaredValueCurrencyOptions();
        commodityUnitValueCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceDiscountCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceFreightCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceInsuranceFeeCurrencyOptions();


        $(document).ready(function () {
            filterPickupPaymentType();
        });

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]', 'click', function (event) {
                var list = ['PAY_BY_SHIPPER_ACCOUNT'];
                var element = '[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option';
                replaceOptionValues(list, element);
            });
        }
        //var currencies = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        //setCurrency(currencies);
    }

// declaredValueCurrencyOptions() // returns void
    function declaredValueCurrencyOptions()
    {
        var list = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        var element = '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueAmount.Currency"] option';
        setCurrencyOptions(list, element);
    }

    {

    }

    }

// invoiceInsuranceFeeCurrencyOptions() // returns void
    function invoiceInsuranceFeeCurrencyOptions()
    {
        var list = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        var element = '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].InvoiceInsuranceFee.Currency"] option';
        setCurrencyOptions(list, element);
    }

// setCurrencyOptions(list, element) // returns void
function setCurrencyOptions(list, element)
    {
        var interval = setInterval(function() 
            {
                var currencies = $(element);
                if (currencies.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function(){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
    {
    this.vm.shipMode = 0;
    this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
    filterPickupPaymentType();

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            var list = ['Pay by shipper account'];            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var currencies = $('[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option');
                if (currencies.length) {
                    debugger;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function (){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
        }
}

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

    //debugger;

    //Map Store Number to ShipperReference
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = nameaddress.Code;

    //Set Default Services Based on From and To Countries		
    var fromCountry = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country;
    var toCountry = nameaddress.Country;

    //Email Address Mappings
	if(nameaddress.Email != null)
	{
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
	}

    //Store Address Book ID value in MiscReference20 to signify that consignee address came from Address Book and was not manually entered.
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = nameaddress.AddressBookId.toString();


    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.GND")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}
}

// SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns void
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns void
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

// function Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function () {
        
         var userContext = client.userContext;
          this.vm.loadVendorConsignee = function () {
            console.log(this.profile.UserInformation);
           
            this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress = {
                
                Company: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Company,
                Contact: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Contact,
                Address1: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Address1,
                Address2: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Address2,
                Address3: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Address3,
                City: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.City,
                StateProvince: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.StateProvince,
                PostalCode: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.PostalCode,
                Country: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Country,
                Email: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Email,
                Phone: this.profile.UserInformation.Address.Phone
            }
            
            var consigneeaddress = consigneeAddress(); 
               
           this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {

                Company: consigneeaddress[0].Company,
                Contact: consigneeaddress[0].Contact,
                Address1: consigneeaddress[0].Address1,
                Address2: consigneeaddress[0].Address2,
                Address3: consigneeaddress[0].Address3,
                City: consigneeaddress[0].City,
                StateProvince: consigneeaddress[0].StateProvince,
                PostalCode: consigneeaddress[0].PostalCode,
                Country: consigneeaddress[0].Country,
                Email: consigneeaddress[0].Email,
                Phone: consigneeaddress[0].Phone,
                Account : consigneeaddress[0].Account
            }
            
            var shipper =  $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val();
            shipper = shipper.replace('string:', '');
           debugger;
            if(shipper !== '' && shipper !== 'SCH_FARGO'){
            
               this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
               
               var thirdpartybillingaddress = thirdPartyBillingAddress(); 
               
               this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {
    
                    Company: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Company,
                    Contact: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Contact,
                    Address1: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Address1,
                    Address2: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Address2,
                    Address3: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Address3,
                    City: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].City,
                    StateProvince: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].StateProvince,
                    PostalCode: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].PostalCode,
                    Country: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Country,
                    Email: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Email,
                    Phone: thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Phone,
                    Account : thirdpartybillingaddress[0].Account
                }
            }
            else
            {
                this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = false;
            }
            
        }
    }

// Source: Schenker, Inc (schenker)_Schenker CBR 2.3 Fix_1756.cs
// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);

        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: 'Cost Center is invalid from User Custom Data', errorCode: '001' });
        }

        if (pageLoaded) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired
            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
        }
    };

// function setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement() // returns undefined
    function setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement() {
        var isRequired = vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'US';
        if (!isRequired) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = false;

            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
            descriptionLabel.css('color', '#337ab7');

            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired;
            consigneePhoneLabel.css('color', '#337ab7');
            consigneePhone.css('border-color', 'rgb(169,68,66)');

        } else {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;

            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = false;
            descriptionLabel.css('color', '#333333');

            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = false;
            consigneePhoneLabel.css('color', '#333333');
            consigneePhone.css('border-color', 'rgb(204,204,204)');

        }
    }

    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

		debugger;
   
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol == "CONNECTSHIP_ROADIE.ROADIE.SD")
            {
                var today = new Date();
		        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference13 = today.toLocaleDateString();    
                var tomorrow = new Date(today);
                tomorrow.setDate(today.getDate() + 1)
                debugger;
                //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.DropOffAppointmentTime = "15:00";
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SpecialDelivery = true;
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery)
                {shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CarrierInstructions = "Recovery mission - gold accomplished!"}
                else
                {shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CarrierInstructions = "Treasure hunt level - scuba required!"};
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].EarliestDeliveryDate = {Month: tomorrow.getMonth()+1, Day: tomorrow.getDate(), Year: tomorrow.getFullYear()};
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].EarliestDeliveryTime = '08:00';
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].LatestDeliveryDate = {Month: tomorrow.getMonth()+1, Day: tomorrow.getDate(), Year: tomorrow.getFullYear()};
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].LatestDeliveryTime = '17:00';
                debugger;
                
            };
        debugger;

    }

  async LoadSampleData()
  {
    let that = this;

    //{
    let Sample = new SampleData();

    //where CSshipper is the order number.  Get the unique orders here and then add them to the select box.
    //when an option is selected, get all corresponding orders from the global OrderJson object
    let uniqueOrders = [...new Set(orders)];

    let sel = $('select[event=SelectOrderFromJson');
    let options = '';
    uniqueOrders.forEach(order =>
    {
      options += `<option value="${order}">${order}</option>`;
    });

    $(sel).append(options);

    //let optAddBulk = '<option value="AddMultiple">Add Multiple Items</option>';
    //let optRemoveBulk = '<option value="RemoveMultiple">Remove Multiple Items</option>';

    //$(sel.append(optAddBulk, optRemoveBulk));

    //put the event handler in here
    $(sel).on('change', function(e)
    {
      $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('hide');

      let v = $(this).val();
      $('.panel-heading-container [sos-key=OrderNumber]').text(v);

      //if (v == 'AddMultiple')
      //{
      //  that.ShowMultipleOperationsDialog(false);
      //  return;
      //}

      //  return;
      //}

      //$('.well').fadeOut().promise().done(function()
      //{
      let o = that.OrderJson.filter(order => order.CSshipper.trim() == v);
      //  //that.AddOrderDataToScreen(o);
      that.CreateOrderTable(o);

      //});
    });

    //});

// Source: SPEEDTECH (SPEEDTECH)_SpeedTech Client Side Business Rules_1645.cs
// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        
        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	       		return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

// DrawDataInReturnForm() // returns void
    function DrawDataInReturnForm(){
        var carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod = 5;
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val(RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION);
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", true);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq('+ carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod +')').prop('selected', true);
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val(shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
    }

// MarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
    function MarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = true;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION;             
        }
    }

// UnMarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
    function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = false;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = undefined;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = '';
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = '';
        }
    }

// Source: Standard Industries (STANDARDINDUSTRIES)_GAF_CBR_2457.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
       debugger;
       if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === null){
           if(!shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery){
              var userName = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.Contact;
              //alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper);
              var theShippers = this.vm.profile.Shippers;
              theShippers.forEach(shpr => {
                  if (shpr.Symbol === shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper) {
                      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {
                        Contact: userName,
                        Company: shpr.Company,
                        Address1: shpr.Address1,
                        Address2: shpr.Address2,
                        Address3: shpr.Address3,
                        City: shpr.City,
                        StateProvince: shpr.StateProvince,
                        PostalCode: shpr.PostalCode,
                        Country: shpr.Country,
                        Phone: shpr.Phone
                    };
                }
            });
          }
       }    
       
    };

// Source: Sun Communities (SUNCOMMUNITIES)_SUN_Business Rules Kiosk_1600.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        var originCustomData = GetCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData) + "-" + GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData) + "," + GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);        
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('TMID', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);                
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = GetKeyValue('DEPARTMENT', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Code = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        var location = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        // MOS or MOO to switch shipper to main office 
        if(location == "MOS" || location == "MOO")
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "MOS";
    };

            else

                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode = 0;                

                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage = "";              

            }
          }
    }

// Source: Sysco Foods (SYSCO)_Client Side Business Rules 20240808_2450.cs
// function customGetWeight() // returns void
function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                    vm.checkShip();                    
                }
            }
        }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping, ConsolidatedOpportunities, OpportunityLoaded) // returns string
function CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping,ConsolidatedOpportunities,OpportunityLoaded)
    {
        var jsonObject = {};
        jsonObject["IsConsolidatedShipping"] = IsConsolidatedShipping;
        jsonObject["ConsolidatedOpportunities"] = ConsolidatedOpportunities.split(',');
        jsonObject["OpportunityLoaded"] = OpportunityLoaded;
        return JSON.stringify(jsonObject);
    }

// shipping() // returns void
        function shipping() {
            vm.AddReturnLabel = function () {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.push(getPackageObject());
            vm.totalPackages = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length;
            };

            vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function () {
                debugger;
                vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND" };
                if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                    vm.selectedServices = [];
                }
                vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };
            

            function getPackageObject() {
                debugger;
                let addedPackage = structuredClone(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0]);
                addedPackage.ReturnDelivery = true;
                addedPackage.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
                return addedPackage;
            };

        }

// Source: Texas EZ Corp (TexasEZ)_Texas EZ Reference Configuration Rule_1595.cs
// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns void
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;

        if (stateProvince == 'PR') {
            nameAddress.Country = 'PR';
        }
        else {
            nameAddress.Country = 'US';
        }
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams){
        /*var consigneeAddress = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        var userAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
        if(consigneeAddress.Country!=userAddress.Country)
        {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Exporter = userAddress
        }*/
        
        var ret = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8);;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg)
        {
            if(pkg.MiscReference7)
            {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages.length > 1 ) {
                    throw ({message: 'Multiple Packages Not Support with Dry Ice', errorCode: ''});
                }

                if (returnPropertyValue(pkg.MiscReference8) === '')
                {
                    throw ({message: 'Missing Dry Ice Weight', errorCode: ''});
                }
                var DryIceWeight = {
                    "Amount": ret.replace('kgs',''),
                    "Units": "KG"
                };
				pkg.DryIceWeight = DryIceWeight;
				
				var Country = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country;
				console.log(Country);
				if(Country =="US"){
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 1;
				}else{
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
				}
				
                pkg.DryIcePurpose = 2;
            }
        });
    }

// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        var shipToEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
        var shipFromEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Email);
        var ref1 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);
        var ref2 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2);
        var ref3 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
        var ref4 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4);
        var ref5 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5);
        var ref6 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6);
        var ref7 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7);
        var ref8 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8);

        var shipperRef = ref1 + "~" + ref2 + "~" + ref3 + "~" + ref4;
        var consigneeRef = ref5 + "~" + ref6;//ref7 + "~" + ref8 + "~" +

        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg)
        {
            if(pkg.MiscReference7)
            {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages.length > 1 ) {
                    throw ({message: 'Multiple Packages Not Support with Dry Ice', errorCode: ''});
                }

                if (returnPropertyValue(pkg.MiscReference8) === '')
                {
                    throw ({message: 'Missing Dry Ice Weight', errorCode: ''});
                }
                
                var ret = ref8;
                
                var DryIceWeight = {
                    "Amount": ret.replace('kgs',''),
                    "Units": "KG"
                };
				pkg.DryIceWeight = DryIceWeight;
				
				var Country = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country;
				console.log(Country);
				if(Country =="US"){
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 1;
				}else{
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
				}
                pkg.DryIcePurpose = 2;
            }
            pkg.ShipperReference = shipperRef;
            pkg.ConsigneeReference = consigneeRef;
            pkg.MiscReference20 = userContext.UserId;

            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = '';
            pkg.ShipNotificationEmail = shipToEmail != '' || shipFromEmail != '';
            if (shipToEmail != '') {
                pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipToEmail;
            }

            if (shipFromEmail != '' ) {
                if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + shipFromEmail;
                } else {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipFromEmail;
                }
            }
        });
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        vm = this.vm;
        //shipmentRequest.CreateShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);

// function GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
    this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }
        if (customDataType === "To") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// Source: Victra (Victra)_Victra Reference Configuration_18.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
      
        //retreive custom user data for Shipper Reference based on CustomData key 
        var customName1 = "Custom1";
        var customName2 = "Custom2";
        var customName3 = "Custom3";
        var customName4 = "Custom4";
        
        var customValue1, customValue2, customValue3, customValue4;
        var CustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        
        if(!CustomData){
            customValue1 = "";
            customValue2 = "";
            customValue3 = "";
            customValue4 = "";
        }else{
        
            for(var Custom in CustomData){
                if(CustomData[Custom].Key==customName1)customValue1 = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                if(CustomData[Custom].Key==customName2)customValue2 = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                if(CustomData[Custom].Key==customName3)customValue3 = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                if(CustomData[Custom].Key==customName4)customValue4 = CustomData[Custom].Value;
            }
        }
        
        //set the above values for first package in the shipment
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = customValue1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customValue2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = customValue3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = customValue4;
           
        
    }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    var consigneeCode = $('select[ng-model="xConsigneeCode"]');
    var selectCode = consigneeCode.val().substring(7);

    if (selectCode === '')
    {
      throw ({ message: 'Please select a lab', errorCode: 43770 });
    }
    var arr = this.vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes;
    var obj = arr.filter(function(nameaddress)
    {
      if (nameaddress.Code === selectCode) { return nameaddress; }
    });

    if (obj.length)
    {
      var nameaddress = obj[0];
      var consignee = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
      consignee.Company = nameaddress.Company;
      consignee.Contact = nameaddress.Contact;
      consignee.Address1 = nameaddress.Address1;
      consignee.Address2 = nameaddress.Address2;
      consignee.Address3 = nameaddress.Address3;
      consignee.City = nameaddress.City;
      consignee.StateProvince = nameaddress.StateProvince;
      consignee.PostalCode = nameaddress.PostalCode;
      consignee.Country = nameaddress.Country;
      consignee.Phone = nameaddress.Phone;
      consignee.Email = nameaddress.Email;
      consignee.Account = nameaddress.Account;

      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = GetKeyValue('shipper', nameaddress.CustomData);
      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince.toUpperCase();
    }
  };

      consignee.Contact = nameaddress.Contact;

      consignee.Address2 = nameaddress.Address2;
      consignee.Address3 = nameaddress.Address3;
      consignee.City = nameaddress.City;
      consignee.StateProvince = nameaddress.StateProvince;
      consignee.PostalCode = nameaddress.PostalCode;

    }
  };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest);
        //var userId = userContext.UserId;
        var ConsigneeCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        var ref1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', ConsigneeCustomData);
        var ref2 = GetKeyValue('Custom2', ConsigneeCustomData);
        var ref3;
        var account = GetKeyValue('Custom3', ConsigneeCustomData);
        //Begin Determine Shipper
        if (account === "0000A0031E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER_A0031E";
        }
        if (account === "0000A0027E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER";
        }
        if (account === "0000872A2E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER_872A2E";
        }
        if (account === "000033A17X") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "AUS";
        }
        if (account === "00007W7182") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "UK";
        }
        if (account === "00005R86R0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "SG_5R86R0";
        }
        if (account === "00005R852X") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "SG_5R852X";
        }
        //End Determine Shipper
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = ref1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = ref2;
        //Begin Determine Service
        var Code = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Code;
        var SvcIdx = Code.lastIndexOf("-");
        if (SvcIdx === -1) {
            //var Service = { "Symbol": "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS Adapter)" };
            var Service = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = Service;
        } else {
            var ServiceCode = Code.substring(SvcIdx + 1, SvcIdx + 2);
            if (ServiceCode === "E") {
                //var ServiceE = { "Symbol": "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS Adapter)" };
                var ServiceE = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = ServiceE;
            }
            if (ServiceCode === "S") {
                //var ServiceS = { Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER", "Name": "UPS Saver (UPS Adapter)"  };
                var ServiceS = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = ServiceS;
            }
        }
        //End Determine Service
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = ref1;
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1) {
                ref3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1;
            } else {
                ref3 = "";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = ref2 + " " + ref3;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference19 = userId;
        }
    };

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.buildShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        this.vm.getUserContext = this.GetUserContext;
        this.vm.postalCodeLookup = this.PostalCodeLookup;

        shipmentRequest.selectAddress = this.SelectAddress;

// UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns undefined
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress == undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;
    }
